  <script>
   // this is the autocomplete for the search - an expanded form because I needed to pass an extra parameter - the imprint code - to limit the search
   $(document).ready(function() {
   
   
    $("input#select-search").autocomplete({
		
	minLength: 2,
	   source: function(request, response) {
	   
	
	
var imprint_code = "1";

            $.ajax({
                url: "search_query.php",
                dataType: "json",
                data: {
                    term: request.term,
                    imprint : imprint_code
                },
                success: function(data) {
                    response(data);
                  
                    
                //   alert(data.length);
                console.log(data);
                
                }
            });
        },
		
focus: function( event, ui ) {
       $( "#select-search" ).val( ui.item.value );
        return false;
      },
select: function( event, ui ) {

/* this is to accommodate those times when the alt_title is being used - it sets the right url for the search - actually this is unnecessary as the alt_title is passed as value, so commented out */

/*
       alt_title = ui.item.alt_title;
       use_alt_title = ui.item.use_alt_title;       
       if ( (alt_title.length > '0') && (use_alt_title=='y') )
       {
       $( "#select-search" ).val( ui.item.alt_title );
       }
else
{
*/

       $( "#select-search" ).val( ui.item.value );
 /*      
       }
       
 */      
        $( "#newbox" ).val( ui.item.id );
        $( "#bookcount" ).val( ui.item.bookcount);
        book_imprint = ui.item.book_imprint;
        author_imprint = ui.item.author_imprint;

	//	$( "#searchsubmit" ).effect('pulsate', {times:10}, 3000);
	
// this below sets the url for the search result - $imprint_url is set at the top of this page

var imprint_url = "http://www.noexit.co.uk/index1.php?imprint=1";

//alert(alt_title);

if ( (book_imprint == '1') || (author_imprint =='1') )
{
imprint_url = "http://www.noexit.co.uk/index1.php?imprint=1";
}
else if ( (book_imprint == '2') || (author_imprint =='2') )
{
imprint_url = "http://www.pocketessentials.co.uk/index1.php?imprint=2";
}

else if ( (book_imprint == '3') || (author_imprint =='3') )
{
imprint_url = "http://www.kamerabooks.co.uk/index1.php?imprint=3";
}


else if ( (book_imprint == '4') || (author_imprint =='4') )
{
imprint_url = "http://www.kamerabooks.co.uk/index1.php?imprint=4";
}

else if ( (book_imprint == '5') || (author_imprint =='5') )
{
imprint_url = "http://www.oldcastlebooks.co.uk/index1.php?imprint=5";
}

else if ( (book_imprint == '6') || (author_imprint =='6') )
{
imprint_url = "http://www.highstakespublishing.co.uk/index1.php?imprint=6";
}

else if ( (book_imprint == '8') || (author_imprint =='8') )
{
imprint_url = "http://www.pulptheclassics.com/index1.php?imprint=8";
}


if ( $( "#bookcount" ).val() > '1' )

{

thissearchterm = $( "#select-search" ).val();


var newurl = (imprint_url + '&term='+thissearchterm+'&search=yes');

window.location.href= newurl;
}

else

{
 
var thenumber = $("#newbox").val();

//alert(thenumber);

var author = "author";

var thistitle = "title";

var ebook = "ebook";

// the autocomplete returns data which is stored in the hidden field called 'newbox' - this data is set as the variable 'thenumber' and includes either 'author' +  author id or 'title' + the isbn


// 'indexof' searches thenumber for the text included in the brackets - if it doesn't find it, it returns -1
if(thenumber.indexOf(author) != -1) 
{
 thelink ="&thisauthorid=";
  
// having identified the content of thenumber as being author related, this strips out the 'author' element, leaving the relevant author_id
  var toRemove = 'author ';
thenumber = thenumber.replace(toRemove,'');
  
  }

  else if (thenumber.indexOf(thistitle) != -1)
  {
  thelink ="&isbn=";
  
    var toRemove = 'title ';
thenumber = thenumber.replace(toRemove,'');
  
  }

   else if (thenumber.indexOf(ebook) != -1)
  {
  thelink ="&isbn=&ebookid=";
  
//alert(thelink);
  
    var toRemove = 'ebook ';
thenumber = thenumber.replace(toRemove,'');
  
  }
  
  

  
var submitvalue = (thelink + thenumber);

//alert(imprint_url + submitvalue);

var newurl = (imprint_url + submitvalue);

window.location.href= newurl;

//$("#searchform").attr("action", imprint_url + submitvalue);
	
	
	
//$( "#searchsubmit" ).css({"color": "#33f"});

}
 
        return false;
      } 
		
          
  }).keypress(function(e) {

          if (e.keyCode === 13) 
          {
            $(this).closest('form').trigger('submit');
          }
          });

});
  </script>
  <script>
   // this is the autocomplete for the mobile search - an expanded form because I needed to pass an extra parameter - the imprint code - to limit the search
   $(document).ready(function() {
   
   
    $("input#mobile-select-search").autocomplete({
		
	minLength: 2,
	   source: function(request, response) {
	   
	
	
var imprint_code = "1";

            $.ajax({
                url: "search_query.php",
                dataType: "json",
                data: {
                    term: request.term,
                    imprint : imprint_code
                },
                success: function(data) {
                    response(data);
                }
            });
        },
		
focus: function( event, ui ) {
        $( "#mobile-select-search" ).val( ui.item.value );
        return false;
      },
select: function( event, ui ) {
        $( "#mobile-select-search" ).val( ui.item.value );
        $( "#mobilenewbox" ).val( ui.item.id );
        $( "#mobilebookcount" ).val( ui.item.bookcount);        
	//	$( "#searchsubmit" ).effect('pulsate', {times:10}, 3000);
	
// this below sets the url for the search result - $imprint_url is set at the top of this page

var imprint_url = "http://www.noexit.co.uk/index1.php?imprint=1";

if ( $( "#mobilebookcount" ).val() > '1' )

{

thissearchterm = $( "#mobile-select-search" ).val();


var newurl = (imprint_url + '&term='+thissearchterm+'&search=yes');

window.location.href= newurl;
}

else

{

 
var thenumber = $("#mobilenewbox").val();

//alert(thenumber);

var author = "author";

var thistitle = "title";

var ebook = "ebook";

// the autocomplete returns data which is stored in the hidden field called 'newbox' - this data is set as the variable 'thenumber' and includes either 'author' +  author id or 'title' + the isbn


// 'indexof' searches thenumber for the text included in the brackets - if it doesn't find it, it returns -1
if(thenumber.indexOf(author) != -1) 
{
 thelink ="&thisauthorid=";
  
// having identified the content of thenumber as being author related, this strips out the 'author' element, leaving the relevant author_id
  var toRemove = 'author ';
thenumber = thenumber.replace(toRemove,'');
  
  }

  else if (thenumber.indexOf(thistitle) != -1)
  {
  thelink ="&isbn=";
  
    var toRemove = 'title ';
thenumber = thenumber.replace(toRemove,'');
  
  }

   else if (thenumber.indexOf(ebook) != -1)
  {
  thelink ="&isbn=&ebookid=";
  
//alert(thelink);
  
    var toRemove = 'ebook ';
thenumber = thenumber.replace(toRemove,'');
  
  }

  
var submitvalue = (thelink + thenumber);

//alert(imprint_url + submitvalue);

var newurl = (imprint_url + submitvalue);

window.location.href= newurl;

//$("#searchform").attr("action", imprint_url + submitvalue);
	
	
	
//$( "#searchsubmit" ).css({"color": "#33f"});


}
 
        return false;
      } 
		
          
  }).keypress(function(e) {

          if (e.keyCode === 13) 
          {
            $(this).closest('form').trigger('submit');
          }
          });

});

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function() {

test_width = $(window).width();
test_height = $(window).height();

popup_height = $('#newsletter_pop_up').outerHeight(true);

popup_width = $('#newsletter_pop_up').outerWidth(true);

this_height = (test_height - popup_height -100);
this_width = (test_width - popup_width - 10);


var query = Modernizr.mq('(max-device-width: 480px)');
if(query) {
position_left = "10"; 
}
else
{
position_left = "20";
}


//alert(position_left);

if(! checkCookie() ) {

var this_ip_address = null;

  setTimeout(function () {


if (position_left =="20")

{


                // Triggering bPopup when click event is fired
                $('#newsletter_pop_up').bPopup({
 
             position:[this_width,this_height], 
                opacity: 0.25,
                closeClass: 'newsletter_close',
               modal: false,
               transition: 'fadein',
               speed: 2000,
              positionStyle: 'absolute',
               zindex: 999
                 
                });
 }
 
else if (position_left =="10")
{

// this is for mobiles

                // Triggering bPopup when click event is fired
                $('#newsletter_pop_up').bPopup({
  
 //postion: ["auto", "auto"],
                opacity: 0.25,
                closeClass: 'newsletter_close',
               modal: false,
               transition: 'fadein',
               speed: 2000                 
                });
 } 
 






$.get("http://ipinfo.io", function(response) {

var referrer = document.referrer;

var website = $(location).attr('href');
var this_ip_address = (response.ip);
var this_company = (response.org);
var this_country = (response.country);
var this_city = (response.city);

var title_tag = $(document).find("title").text();

//alert(this_country);

$.post("popup_tracking_data.php", { website:website, ip_address:this_ip_address, company:this_company, country:this_country, city:this_city, title:title_tag, referring_site: referrer  },
			function(result){

		});

}, "jsonp");


 
   }, 20000);
   
   
            
      
setCookie("popup", "visitor", 1);
}



function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {

var d = new Date();
d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();

document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + "; " + expires;
}

function getCookie(cname) {
var name = cname + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
if (c.indexOf(name) != -1) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
}
return "";
}

function checkCookie() {
var user = getCookie("popup");
if (user != "") 
{
return true;
} 
else 
{
return false;
}
}


});

var this_ip_address = (response.ip);

//alert(website);

$.post("popup_tracking_data.php", { update_website:website, update_ip_address:this_ip_address },
			function(result){

		});

		}, "jsonp");

	
	});

});

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function togglepublicity(showHideDiv, switchTextDiv) {
	var ele = document.getElementById(showHideDiv);
	var text = document.getElementById(switchTextDiv);
	if(ele.style.display == "block") {
    		ele.style.display = "none";
	
//		text.innerHTML = ("Show PR Email");
  	}
	else {
		ele.style.display = "block";
//		text.innerHTML = ('Hide PR Email');
	}
}
  </script>
  <script>
   $(document).ready(function(){

$('.publicity_data').click(function() {

identifier = $(this).attr('identifier');

hideorshow = $(this).text();

//alert(hideorshow);

if(hideorshow.indexOf('Show') >= 0)
{
newhideorshow = hideorshow.replace('Show', 'Hide');
}

if(hideorshow.indexOf('Hide') >= 0)
{
newhideorshow = hideorshow.replace('Hide', 'Show');
}
    

$(this).text(newhideorshow);



this_url = 'publicity_data_content.php?this_id='+identifier;

    $.ajax({
       url: this_url,
       success: function(html) {
      
        $('div[id="publicitybox'+identifier+'"]').append(html);
          
 //    alert("yes");
       }
    });
 
});

});
  </script>

$(".small_price").html(multiplier+"print &pound;"+tpb_discount_price);

combined_price = (parseFloat(multiple_price) + parseFloat(ebook_price));
combined_price = combined_price.toFixed(2);
$(".combined_price").html('<span style=\"text-decoration: line-through; color: #333; font-size: 1.5em;\">&pound;'+combined_price+'</span> <span style=\"color: #f00; font-size: 1.5em;\"> &pound;'+multiple_price+'</span>');
}
else
{
multiple_price = ( quantity_box_value * parseFloat(tpb_price) );
multiple_price = multiple_price.toFixed(2);
$(".small_price").html(multiplier+"print &pound;:"+tpb_price);
$(".item_price").html(offer_message+ " Total: &pound" + multiple_price);

combined_price = (parseFloat(multiple_price) + parseFloat(ebook_price));
combined_price = combined_price.toFixed(2);

$(".combined_price").html('<span style=\"text-decoration: line-through; color: #333; font-size: 1.5em;\">&pound;'+combined_price+'</span> <span style=\"color: #f00; font-size: 1.5em;\"> &pound;'+multiple_price+'</span>');

}

$(".item_price").html("&pound;" + multiple_price);

         // DOM Ready
        $(function() {

            // Binding a click event
            // From jQuery v.1.7.0 use .on() instead of .bind()
            $('.tandc').on('click', function(e) {

                // Prevents the default action to be triggered. 
                e.preventDefault();

                // Triggering bPopup when click event is fired
                $('.buy_range').bPopup({
                opacity: 0.25,
                closeClass: 'close'
                });

            });

        });

    })(jQuery);

  function(data) {
  $('#buy_range').append(data);
                 // Triggering bPopup when click event is fired 
  $('.buy_range').bPopup({
                opacity: 0.25,
                closeClass: 'close',
                
//this function replaces the content of the div that's popped up with the basic stuff - otherwise the book links from previous clicks also appear                
                onClose: function(){$('#buy_range').html( "<span class='close'>X</span><p>ORDER NOW FROM ONE OF THESE SUPPLIERS</p>" );}
                
                });
});


                // Prevents the default action to be triggered. 
                e.preventDefault();

            });

        });

    })(jQuery);
  </script>
  <script>
   ;(function($) {

         // DOM Ready
        $(function() {

            // Binding a click event
            // From jQuery v.1.7.0 use .on() instead of .bind()
            $('.merge').on('click', function(e) {
            
            
           year = $(this).attr('name');
           month = $(this).attr('id');
           imprint = $(this).attr('rel');
//           alert (year + month + imprint);

busy = month+year+imprint;

//alert (busy);

$('#'+busy).show();


//  note the order_link_code_new_php has to be in the pocket essentials domain as jquery won't do cross domain queries            
$.post("ai_pdf/newmerge_pdf.php", { year: year, month: month, imprint, imprint },
function(data) {
$('#pdf_link').append(data);
                 // Triggering bPopup when click event is fired 
  $('.buy_range').bPopup({
                opacity: 0.25,
                closeClass: 'close',
                
//this function replaces the content of the div that's popped up with the basic stuff - otherwise the book links from previous clicks also appear                
                onClose: function(){$('#pdf_link').html( "<span class='close'>X</span><p>COMBINED PDFS FOR THE FOLLOWING TITLES:</p>" );}
                
                });
$('#'+busy).hide();      
});


                // Prevents the default action to be triggered. 
                e.preventDefault();

            });

        });

    })(jQuery);
  </script>
  <script>
   ;(function($) {

         // DOM Ready
        $(function() {

            // Binding a click event
            // From jQuery v.1.7.0 use .on() instead of .bind()
            $('.rocliffe').on('click', function(e) {

                // Prevents the default action to be triggered. 
                e.preventDefault();

                // Triggering bPopup when click event is fired
                $('#rocliffe_launch').bPopup({
                opacity: 0.25,
                closeClass: 'close'
                });

            });

        });

    })(jQuery);
  </script>
